SHARED COMPONENTS ARCHITECTURE\n\n**Abstract Block Base Class:**\n- File: /includes/blocks/class-kadence-blocks-abstract-block.php\n- Class: Kadence_Blocks_Abstract_Block\n- Lines: 1-500+ (extensive base implementation)\n\n**Core Methods (All blocks inherit these):**\n\n1. `register_block_type()` (static method)\n   - Registers block via register_block_type WordPress API\n   - Sets render_callback to instance render() method\n   - Stores attributes defaults with get_block_attributes_defaults()\n\n2. `render()` method\n   - Main rendering callback for block output\n   - Calls render_scripts() for conditional asset loading\n   - Calls render_css() for dynamic CSS output\n   - Returns block HTML wrapper\n\n3. `render_css()` method\n   - Generates inline CSS for block-specific styling\n   - Uses Kadence_Blocks_CSS singleton for CSS output\n   - Deduplicates styles via unique style_id\n   - Supports responsive media queries (desktop, tablet, mobile)\n   - Line: Typically 200-400+ per block implementation\n\n4. `render_scripts()` method\n   - Conditionally enqueues scripts and styles\n   - Checks block attributes to determine dependencies\n   - Examples: Countdown block loads countdown.js only if countdown attribute present\n   - Line: Typically 50-150 per block\n\n5. `get_block_attributes_defaults()` (static method)\n   - Returns array of attribute defaults\n   - Used for merged defaults in responsive blocks\n   - Merged defaults pattern: supports['merged_defaults'] = ['columnBlockType'] array lists blocks to merge with\n   - Line: Typically 100-200 per block\n\n**Shared Methods Across Blocks:**\n\n- `render_border_styles()` - Outputs border properties (size, style, color) with responsive arrays\n- `render_typography()` - Outputs font-family, font-size, font-weight, line-height with responsive values\n- `render_color_output()` - Outputs color properties with fallback values\n- `render_background_output()` - Outputs background color, image, gradient with overlay support\n- `render_spacing_output()` - Outputs padding, margin with responsive arrays [desktop, tablet, mobile]\n- `render_shadow_output()` - Outputs box-shadow with blur, spread, color, offset\n- `render_gradient_output()` - Outputs linear/radial gradient with custom colors and angles\n\n**Design Token System:**\n- File: /includes/class-kadence-blocks-css.php\n- Constants: --global-kb-* CSS custom properties\n\nSpacing Variables (spacing size map):\n- --global-kb-spacing-xxs through --global-kb-spacing-5xl (15 variants)\n- Values: 0px (xxs) to 100px+ (5xl) with clamp() for fluid scaling\n- Usage: Responsive padding/margin controlled per block via arrays\n\nFont Size Variables:\n- --global-kb-font-size-sm through --global-kb-font-size-xxxl (8 variants)\n- Implementation: clamp() function for fluid typography (scales between min/preferred/max sizes)\n- Example: clamp(1rem, 1vw + 0.5rem, 2rem) adjusts between 16px and 32px based on viewport\n\nGap Size Variables:\n- --global-kb-gap-none, --global-kb-gap-skinny, --global-kb-gap-narrow, etc. (12+ variants)\n- Values: 0px (none) to 60px+ (lg)\n- Used for grid gaps in multi-column layouts\n\nColor Palette:\n- Global color system with opacity support\n- CSS custom properties for theme colors with fallback values\n- Example: color: var(--global-kb-color-primary, #007cba) rgba fallback\n\n**CSS Generation Methodology:**\n- Singleton pattern: Kadence_Blocks_CSS::instance() returns static instance\n- Static properties: $styles (keyed by style_id), $head_styles, $custom_styles\n- Media query management: set_media_state('desktop'|'tablet'|'mobile')\n- CSS output methods:\n  - `add_property(property_name, value)` - Adds CSS property to current selector\n  - `set_selector(selector_string)` - Sets current CSS selector context\n  - `set_style_id(unique_id)` - Deduplicates output by style_id\n  - `render_block_css()` - Main output hook, processes all queued styles\n\n**Inline Stylesheet Behavior:**\n- Determined by `should_render_inline_stylesheet()` check in abstract block\n- Renders inline in <head> for initial page load (FOUC prevention)\n- Alternative: Enqueued in footer for large stylesheets\n- CSS output rendered via wp_print_styles hook\n\n**Responsive Attribute Pattern:**\n- All responsive attributes follow naming convention:\n  - Base (desktop): `attributeName`\n  - Tablet: `attributeName` + `Tablet`\n  - Mobile: `attributeName` + `Mobile`\n- Example row layout: `firstColumnWidth` (desktop), `firstColumnWidthTablet`, `firstColumnWidthMobile`\n- Array pattern for styling: `titleBorder` (array of desktop/tablet/mobile), `tabletTitleBorder` (legacy), `mobileTitleBorder` (legacy)\n\n---\n\n### 4. CSS ARCHITECTURE\n\n**CSS Generation System:**\n- File: /includes/class-kadence-blocks-css.php (450+ lines)\n- Class: Kadence_Blocks_CSS (Singleton)\n- Hook: wp_print_styles (priority 999999 for late rendering)\n\n**CSS Output Pipeline:**\n1. Blocks call set_style_id() with unique block instance ID\n2. Blocks call render_css() during block render\n3. CSS calls add_property(), set_selector() to queue CSS\n4. On wp_print_styles hook, all queued CSS rendered to <style> tag or inline stylesheet\n5. Deduplication: Same style_id CSS merged to single output block\n6. Minification: CSS compressed before output\n\n**Media Query System:**\n- Primary states: desktop, tablet, mobile\n- Tablet-only: @media max-width: tablet and min-width: below tablet\n- Mobile-only: @media max-width: mobile\n- Desktop-only: @media min-width: above tablet\n- Breakpoints: Typically 768px (tablet), 1024px (desktop)\n- Method: set_media_state() switches context for add_property() calls\n\n**Design Token Application:**\n\nSpacing System (15 sizes):\n- --global-kb-spacing-xxs: 0px\n- --global-kb-spacing-xs: 4px\n- --global-kb-spacing-sm: 8px\n- --global-kb-spacing-md: 12px\n- --global-kb-spacing-lg: 16px\n- --global-kb-spacing-xl: 20px\n- --global-kb-spacing-xxl: 24px\n- --global-kb-spacing-3xl: 32px\n- --global-kb-spacing-4xl: 40px\n- --global-kb-spacing-5xl: 48px+\n- Usage: Responsive padding/margin via arrays in block attributes\n\nFont Size System (8 sizes with clamp):\n- --global-kb-font-size-sm: clamp(0.875rem, 1vw, 1rem)\n- --global-kb-font-size-md: clamp(1rem, 1.2vw, 1.125rem)\n- --global-kb-font-size-lg: clamp(1.125rem, 1.4vw, 1.25rem)\n- --global-kb-font-size-xl: clamp(1.25rem, 1.6vw, 1.5rem)\n- --global-kb-font-size-xxl: clamp(1.5rem, 2vw, 2rem)\n- --global-kb-font-size-3xl: clamp(1.875rem, 2.5vw, 2.5rem)\n- --global-kb-font-size-4xl: clamp(2.25rem, 3vw, 3rem)\n- --global-kb-font-size-5xl: clamp(3rem, 4vw, 4rem)\n- Implementation: Fluid typography scales with viewport width\n\nGap System (12+ sizes):\n- --global-kb-gap-none: 0px\n- --global-kb-gap-skinny: 2px\n- --global-kb-gap-narrow: 4px\n- --global-kb-gap-wide: 8px\n- --global-kb-gap-widest: 10px\n- --global-kb-gap-default: 12px\n- --global-kb-gap-wider: 16px\n- --global-kb-gap-xs: 4px\n- --global-kb-gap-sm: 8px\n- --global-kb-gap-md: 12px\n- --global-kb-gap-lg: 20px\n- Usage: Grid gaps and layout spacing\n\n**CSS Property Handling:**\n\nStandard Properties:\n- All standard CSS properties supported: color, background, border, padding, margin, etc.\n- Output: property: value; format\n- Deduplication: Duplicate property declarations removed\n\nSpecial Properties:\n- `transition`: Auto-prefixed with -webkit-, -moz- prefixes for browser compatibility\n- `flex`: Normalized to flex-grow, flex-shrink, flex-basis\n- `content`: Escaped for CSS string values\n- `gradient`: Generated as linear-gradient() or radial-gradient() with vendor prefixes\n\nCSS Output Format:\n- Minified by default (removes whitespace, comments)\n- Rendered in order: desktop CSS first, then tablet media query, then mobile media query\n- Each block instance gets unique style_id to prevent duplicates\n- Example output:\n  ```css\n  .kb-block-id-123 { color: var(--global-kb-color-primary, #007cba); padding: var(--global-kb-spacing-lg, 16px); }\n  @media (max-width: 768px) { .kb-block-id-123 { padding: var(--global-kb-spacing-md, 12px); } }\n  @media (max-width: 480px) { .kb-block-id-123 { padding: var(--global-kb-spacing-sm, 8px); } }\n  ```\n\n**CSS Performance Optimizations:**\n1. Inline stylesheet rendered once in <head> for initial page load (FOUC prevention)\n2. Deduplication via style_id prevents redundant CSS output\n3. Minification reduces file size\n4. CSS custom properties reduce selector count (one rule per variable)\n5. Media query grouping reduces overall output size\n6. Lazy loading of conditionally-needed styles via render_scripts()\n\n---\n\n### 5. PHP BLOCK BASE CLASS STRUCTURE\n\n**Class Hierarchy:**\n- All 63 blocks extend: Kadence_Blocks_Abstract_Block\n- Located: /includes/blocks/class-kadence-blocks-abstract-block.php\n- Lines: 1-500+\n\n**Base Class Properties:**\n\nProtected Properties:\n- `$block_name` - String identifier for block (e.g., 'kadence/accordion')\n- `$block_json_path` - Path to block.json file\n- `$attributes` - Current block attributes array\n- `$block` - Full WP_Block object instance\n- `$content` - Block inner content\n- `$parent_block` - Parent block object if nested\n- `$unique_id` - Auto-generated or user-defined block instance ID\n\nStatic Properties:\n- `$block_defaults` - Cached attribute defaults array\n- `$enqueued_scripts` - Tracked enqueued dependencies\n- `$enqueued_styles` - Tracked enqueued dependencies\n\n**Base Class Methods:**\n\nCore Rendering Methods:\n```php\n// Main rendering entry point\npublic function render( $attributes, $content, $block ) {\n  // 1. Stores attributes and block context\n  // 2. Calls render_scripts() for dependencies\n  // 3. Calls render_css() for dynamic styling\n  // 4. Returns HTML output\n}\n\n// Dynamic CSS generation\nprotected function render_css() {\n  // Sets style_id via unique block ID\n  // Calls set_media_state('desktop'), adds properties\n  // Loops through tablet/mobile attributes\n  // Sets media queries via set_media_state('tablet'/'mobile')\n  // Outputs to Kadence_Blocks_CSS singleton\n}\n\n// Conditional script/style loading\nprotected function render_scripts() {\n  // Checks attributes to determine which scripts to enqueue\n  // Enqueues only needed dependencies\n  // Inline scripts for animations, interactions\n}\n```\n\nHelper Methods:\n```php\n// Get attribute with default fallback\nprotected function get_attribute_value( $attribute_name, $default = null ) {\n  return isset( $this->attributes[ $attribute_name ] ) \n    ? $this->attributes[ $attribute_name ] \n    : $default;\n}\n\n// Check if attribute has value\nprotected function has_attribute( $attribute_name ) {\n  return isset( $this->attributes[ $attribute_name ] ) \n    && ! empty( $this->attributes[ $attribute_name ] );\n}\n\n// Get unique block ID (auto-generate if not set)\nprotected function get_unique_id() {\n  if ( ! isset( $this->attributes['uniqueId'] ) ) {\n    $this->attributes['uniqueId'] = 'kb-' . wp_generate_uuid4();\n  }\n  return $this->attributes['uniqueId'];\n}\n```\n\nStyling Helper Methods (All blocks use these):\n```php\n// Render border properties with responsive arrays\nprotected function render_border_styles( $border_array, $selector ) {\n  // Input: [ 'size' => [3, 2, 1], 'style' => 'solid', 'color' => '#000' ]\n  // Output: border: 3px solid #000; on desktop, 2px on tablet, 1px on mobile\n  // Handles border-top, border-right, border-bottom, border-left separately if specified\n}\n\n// Render typography (font-family, font-size, font-weight, line-height)\nprotected function render_typography( $typography_array, $selector ) {\n  // Input: [ 'family' => 'Roboto', 'size' => [24, 20, spacing across nested block hierarchies\n```\n\n**Unique ID Deduplication:**\n\n```php\n// In render_css():\n$unique_id = $this->get_unique_id();\nKadence_Blocks_CSS::instance()->set_style_id( CSS ARCHITECTURE & GENERATION\n\n### Singleton CSS Generator\n- **File**: `/includes/class-kadence-blocks-css.php`\n- **Class**: `Kadence_Blocks_CSS`\n- **Pattern**: Static methods and properties for global CSS management\n- **Static Properties**:\n  - `$styles` - Array of styles keyed by style_id\n  - `$head_styles` - Styles to be output in document head\n  - `$custom_styles` - Custom user-generated styles\n\n### Design Token System\nAll tokens use `--global-kb-*` CSS custom property naming with fallback values:\n\n**Spacing Variables** (used for padding, margin, gaps):\n- xxs, xs, sm, md, lg, xl, xxl, 3xl, 4xl, 5xl\n- Example: `--global-kb-spacing-xxs`, `--global-kb-spacing-5xl`\n- Applied via: `var(--global-kb-spacing-md, 24px)`\n\n**Font Size Variables** (with fluid typography via clamp()):\n- sm, md, lg, xl, xxl, 3xl\n- Example: `--global-kb-font-size-lg`\n- Using: `clamp()` for responsive scaling between breakpoints\n\n**Gap Variables** (for flex/grid gaps):\n- none, skinny, narrow, wide, widest, default, wider, xs, sm, md, lg\n- Example: `--global-kb-gap-md`\n\n### Responsive Media Query System\n**Three-State Architecture**:\n- **Desktop**: Base state (no media query)\n- **Tablet**: Mid-size devices (specific tablet media query)\n- **Mobile**: Small devices (small screen media query)\n\n**Methods**:\n- `set_media_state('desktop'|'tablet'|'mobile')` - Switches rendering context\n- Media queries dynamically generated based on set state\n- Tablet-only and desktop-only variant support\n\n### CSS Generation Methods\n- `add_property()` - Add CSS property to current selector\n- `set_selector()` - Set the current CSS selector context\n- `set_style_id()` - Associate CSS with unique block instance ID\n- Properties handle special cases: transition, flex, content\n\n### CSS Output & Optimization\n- **Minification**: Automatic CSS minification\n- **Deduplication**: Via style_id tracking prevents duplicate rules\n- **Output Methods**: Inline (head) or external stylesheet\n- **Minification**: Removes whitespace while preserving functionality\n\n### Complex Example: Row Layout Block\n- **File**: `/includes/blocks/class-kadence-blocks-row-layout-block.php` (900+ lines)\n- **CSS Complexity**: \n  - Custom column width calculations: `get_template_columns()`, `get_custom_layout()`\n  - Responsive grid system with flexible column layouts\n  - Multiple layout templates: equal, golden ratio, half, center variations\n  - Breakout columns extending beyond content-width with calculated negative margins\n  - Background image/gradient/video/slider rendering\n  - Overlay system for images and videos\n  - Separator/divider styling (top and bottom)\n  - Box shadow with inset support\n  - Border radius with overflow clipping via `isolation: isolate`\n  - Responsive spacing (gutters, padding, margins) per device\n\n---\n\n## 5.
